  --data-path '/content/gdrive/MyDrive/data/ias_assignment_1/Copy_of_images/unzipped' \
  --annotationfile '/content/gdrive/MyDrive/data/ias_assignment_1/Copy_of_images/unzipped/Copy_of_annotations.json' \
